Becoming a Cavirin API consumer

PLACEHOLDER FOR CAVIRIN API CONSUMER DOCUMENTATION

Credentials

The API endpoint for credentials

/settings/credentials get post

get

Returns a collection of credentials

post

Creates a new credential

get /settings/credentials

Returns a collection of credentials

  • Response

HTTP status code 200

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-04/schema#",
  "title": "Credentials",
  "description": "A collection of Credential items",
  "type": "object",
  "properties": {
    "credentials": {
      "type": "array",
      "items": {
        "$ref": "credentialSchema"
      }
    }
  }
}

HTTP status code 401

Not authenticated. This could be due to a missing or invalid Authorization token, which is required to access this resource. See (http://cavirin.com/api/authentication) for more info

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-04/schema#",
  "title": "Error",
  "description": "A common error response",
  "type": "object",
  "properties": {
    "timestamp": {
      "description": "The time of the response",
      "type": "number",
      "format": "int64"
    },
    "status": {
      "description": "The HTTP response status code",
      "type": "integer"
    },
    "error": {
      "description": "The HTTP response description",
      "type": "string"
    },
    "message": {
      "description": "A descriptive message, optionally i18N translated",
      "type": "string"
    },
    "path": {
      "description": "The URI path",
      "type": "string"
    },
    "code": {
      "description": "An application internal string, typically a number but possibly containing other characters. This is provided to aid in helping determine the cause of the problem if needed",
      "type": "string"
    },
    "more_info": {
      "description": "A message to find out more info about the specific error response, typically a link to a web page that details the code property and why this exact response may have occured.",
      "type": "string"
    }
  },
  "required": [
    "status"
  ]
}

HTTP status code 403

Unauthorized. Credentials are correct, but access to this resource is denied. The consumer does not have the permissions to make calls to this resource using this method type.

post /settings/credentials

Creates a new credential

  • Request
  • Response

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-04/schema#",
  "title": "CredentialSchema",
  "description": "A single credential",
  "type": "object",
  "properties": {
    "id": {
      "type": "integer",
      "title": "id"
    },
    "label": {
      "type": "string",
      "title": "label"
    },
    "username": {
      "type": "string",
      "title": "username"
    },
    "password": {
      "type": "string",
      "title": "password"
    },
    "usage": {
      "type": "string",
      "title": "usage"
    },
    "pemFile": {
      "type": "string",
      "title": "pemFile"
    },
    "credentialType": {
      "type": "string",
      "title": "credentialtype"
    },
    "keyPairFilePath": {
      "type": "string",
      "title": "keyPairFilePath"
    },
    "created": {
      "description": "The creation time",
      "type": "integer"
    },
    "modified": {
      "description": "The time of modification",
      "type": "integer"
    },
    "deleted": {
      "description": "The flag to indicate if a particular object is soft deleted or not",
      "type": "boolean"
    }
  }
}

Example:

[{"label":"sample label","username":"sample username","password":"sample password"}]

HTTP status code 201

The request has been fulfilled and resulted in a new resource being created

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-04/schema#",
  "title": "CredentialSchema",
  "description": "A single credential",
  "type": "object",
  "properties": {
    "id": {
      "type": "integer",
      "title": "id"
    },
    "label": {
      "type": "string",
      "title": "label"
    },
    "username": {
      "type": "string",
      "title": "username"
    },
    "password": {
      "type": "string",
      "title": "password"
    },
    "usage": {
      "type": "string",
      "title": "usage"
    },
    "pemFile": {
      "type": "string",
      "title": "pemFile"
    },
    "credentialType": {
      "type": "string",
      "title": "credentialtype"
    },
    "keyPairFilePath": {
      "type": "string",
      "title": "keyPairFilePath"
    },
    "created": {
      "description": "The creation time",
      "type": "integer"
    },
    "modified": {
      "description": "The time of modification",
      "type": "integer"
    },
    "deleted": {
      "description": "The flag to indicate if a particular object is soft deleted or not",
      "type": "boolean"
    }
  }
}

Example:

{"id":"sample id","label":"sample label","loginId":"sample loginId","region":"sample region","accessKey":"sample accessKey","secretAccessKey":"sample secretAccessKey","password":"sample password","credentialtype":"sample credentialtype","keyPairFilePath":"sample keyPairFilePath","pemFile":"sample pemFile"}

  • Response
